***proza.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:proza.html>proza</a> (41679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">prose</i>, the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> word <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōsa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straightforward</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from the term <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōsa ōrātio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a straightforward speech- i.e. without the ornaments of verse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***pruik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pruik.html>pruik</a> (6491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Early modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">peruick</i>/<i>pairuque</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">perruque</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruik.html>pruik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruiken.html>pruiken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruikje.html>pruikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wig, peruke</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pruik.html>pruik</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

***pruim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pruim.html>pruim</a> (21821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prume</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*prūma</i>. A variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*plūma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*plūmā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prūnum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">προῦμνον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proûmnon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Plums.jpg/250px-Plums.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="206" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Plums.jpg/375px-Plums.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Plums.jpg/500px-Plums.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="844" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i>Japanse <a href = vnd.unilang:pruim.html>pruim</a></i><br />Japanese plum</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruim.html>pruim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimpje.html>pruimpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A plum tree, one of certain trees of the genus <i>Prunus</i>, especially <i>Prunus domestica</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pruimenboom</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A plum <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fruit from a plum tree</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<ul><li>Hieronymus <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Alphen, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> pruimeboom".
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eieren.html>eieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a>. / '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheen.html>Scheen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>wou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plukken.html>plukken</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:schoon.html>schoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbood.html>verbood</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Little Jan once saw <b>plums</b> (or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulvas</a></b>; see below) hanging / <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a>! so big as eggs. / it seemed that little Jan <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> going to pluck them / though his father forbade him that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>John <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Mill (<a href = vnd.unilang:johan.html>Johan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Meulen), "Pruimejantje".
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eieren.html>eieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a>; / <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuinman.html>tuinman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bolle.html>bolle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wangen.html>wangen</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:sloeg.html>Sloeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuile.html>vuile</a> gapper <a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">quid</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">piece of chewing tobacco</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulva</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a> (14103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruim.html>pruim</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chew tobacco</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to (like to) eat, to have taste for</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Mainly used in expressions like <i><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prul.html>prul</a> (23043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Prüll</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stuff, junk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prul.html>prul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prullen.html>prullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prulletje.html>prulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a useless or worthless thing; <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the plural:</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> junk, trinket, trifle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nutteloze.html>nutteloze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:prullen.html>prullen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weggooien.html>weggooien</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> have to throw out all that useless junk.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">turd</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:loser.html>loser</a></span>, a useless or unpleasant <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">diminutive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> hypocoristic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">a nickname or an affectionate term for a child, in particular a girl</span></li></ol>

***prut.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>prut</a> (26513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic, presumably a metonym from the sound made by a substance or something falling into it. First attested in early modern Dutch. The same in regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Prütt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>prut</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Sound of a thick, almost-solid substance.</span></li>
<li>cheers
<ul><li><b>2016</b> April 30, Wouter <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Noort, "‘<a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a>’", <i>NRC Handelsblad</i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ondanks.html>Ondanks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> 27 <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verenigde.html>Verenigde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staten.html>Staten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> Rotterdams <a href = vnd.unilang:accent.html>accent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maart.html>Maarten</a> Sierhuis. <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:biertje.html>biertje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonnige.html>zonnige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terras.html>terras</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naast.html>naast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kantoor.html>kantoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middenin.html>middenin</a> San Francisco <a href = vnd.unilang:proost.html>proost</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zegt.html>zegt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> „<b><a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>Prut</a></b>!”</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>prut</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any substance with a thick, gooey or almost-solid consistency, such as:
<ol><li>gunk, mud
<ul><li><b>2015</b> December 11, J. Visscher, "Gemakzucht <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duur.html>duur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a>", <i>Reformatorisch <a href = vnd.unilang:dagblad.html>Dagblad</a></i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afzien.html>afzien</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Veluwse <b><a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>prut</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometers.html>Kilometers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> uitgeputte <a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoot.html>stoot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dierlijke.html>dierlijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klanken.html>klanken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>Langs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> modderpad <a href = vnd.unilang:drukt.html>drukt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloekend.html>vloekend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:tien.html>tien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:instructeur.html>instructeur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijkt.html>kijkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of snow</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1976</b>, Jan Cremer, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuw.html>Sneeuw</a></i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagdelijk.html>Maagdelijk</a> ijskristal <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grauwe.html>grauwe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>prut</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Virgin ice <a href = vnd.unilang:crystals.html>crystals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> into <a href = vnd.unilang:drab.html>drab</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>mash, stew, porridge</li>
<li>grounds (<i>in coffee</i>) or any other thick residue

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:puberaal.html>puberaal</a> (48638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed, cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">puberal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:puberale.html>puberale</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puber.html>puber</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aal</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puberaal.html>puberaal</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Pertaining to puberty; <span class="Latn" lang="en">pubescent</span>, pubertal.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Resembling teenage behaviour; <span class="Latn" lang="en">immature</span>.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:publiceren.html>publiceren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">publicer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pūblicō</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puf.html>puf</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></i>, sharing an imitative <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> base with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">pyffan</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">puff</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to puff, blow out (hot air, such as the chugging of a steam engine)</li></ol>

***pug.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a> (50897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pug_portrait.jpg/220px-Pug_portrait.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pug_portrait.jpg/330px-Pug_portrait.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pug_portrait.jpg/440px-Pug_portrait.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>portrait of a <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small dog of an ancient breed originating in China, having a snub nose, wrinkled face, squarish body, short smooth hair, and curled tail. <span class="defdate">[from the 18th c]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Chinese <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Dutch bulldog</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mini <a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mops.html>mops</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:carlin.html>carlin</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pugdog</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A bargeman. <span class="defdate">[from the 16th c]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chaff; the refuse of grain
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Holland to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any geometrid moth of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Eupithecia" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Eupithecia"><i>Eupithecia</i></a></span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Corruption of <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:puck.html>puck</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">pūca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>goblin</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">púki</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">pwca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hobgoblin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a> or hobgoblin.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Jonson to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>An upper servant in a great house. <span class="defdate">[from the 19th c]</span></li>
<li>A harlot; a prostitute. <span class="defdate">[circa 1600]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Cotgrave to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">mythological creature</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:puck.html>puck</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>goblin</a>, fairy</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pugilist</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pugil</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who <a href = vnd.unilang:fights.html>fights</a> with fists; a boxer.
<ul><li><b>1988</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>Ken</a> Blady, <i>The Jewish <a href = vnd.unilang:boxers.html>Boxers</a> Hall of Fame</i> (page 226)
<dl><dd>He never trained for his characters either: with his slurred speech and disfigured mug he usually portrayed a punch-drunk <a href = vnd.unilang:ex-.html>ex-</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></b> or comic tough guy, roles in which he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a natural.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">pucken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thump, beat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any compressed clay-like material mixed and worked into a soft, plastic condition for making <a href = vnd.unilang:bricks.html>bricks</a>, pottery or for paving. (Also <i><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a> soil</i>)</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a> mill.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pugging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pugged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To mix and stir when <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> for <a href = vnd.unilang:bricks.html>bricks</a> or pottery</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fill or <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> with <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> by tamping; to fill in or spread with mortar, as a floor or partition, for the purpose of deadening sound.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">पग</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pag</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">step, foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पद्य</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">padya</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">πόδι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pódi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The pawprint or footprint of an animal</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pugmark</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology 6</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably related to <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:puck.html>puck</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">A term of <a href = vnd.unilang:endearment.html>endearment</a>.</span> <span class="defdate">[from the 16th c]</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:puimsteen.html>puimsteen</a> (80214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puimsteen.html>puimsteen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puimsteen.html>puimstenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puimsteen.html>puimsteentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:puimsteen.html>puimsteen</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:puls.html>puls</a> (26972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pulse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pulsus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puls.html>puls</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pulsen.html>pulsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puls.html>pulsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pulse (e.g. of a shock, heartbeat or <a href = vnd.unilang:sonar.html>sonar</a>).</li></ol>

***pulsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pulsen.html>pulsen</a> (44806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from the name of a moving company Abraham <a href = vnd.unilang:puls.html>Puls</a> amp; Sons, employed by the Nazi-led Dutch police to pillage and empty the homes of the 140,000 Jews of the Netherlands during the Holocaust.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pulsen.html>pulsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to violently dispossess, to loot, to destroy property and environment, of Jews in particular.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
